. *program drop InvalidIV_ATEw

. # delimit ;
delimiter now ;
. set more 1;

. program InvalidIV_ATEw, eclass;
  1. /* Calculate Bounds on ATE and ATT with an Invalid IV*/;
. /* Calculate a normalized weight,wgt*/;
.         marksample touse;
  2.         args y z s wgt sv;
  3.         confirm var `y' `z' `s' `wgt' `sv';
  4.           /* syntax: depvar treatmentvar selectvar wgt sortvar */;
.                           /* depvar is the outcome variable */;
.                           /* treatmentvar is the binary treatment variable */;
.                           /* selectvar is the binary sample selection indicator */;
.                           /* wei1 is the design weight */;
.                           /* sortvar is the variable that will break "ties" if the outcome variable is discrete */;
.                                 tempvar y_trim1 y_trim0 swgt1 swgt0;
  5.  /* outcomevar to be trimmed, accumulative weights in {Z=1,D=1} and {Z=0,D=0}*/;
.     tempname pr_at_c pr_nt_c;
  6.         tempvar at nt at_c nt_c;
  7.  /* principal strata indicator*/;
.         tempvar upid_at lowid_at upid_c1 lowid_c1 upid_nt lowid_nt upid_c0 lowid_c0;
  8.  /* unconstrained upper and lower bound indicators*/;
.         tempname sumw1 sumw0 ;
  9.  /* sum of weights in {Z=1,D=1} and {Z=0,D=0} */;
.                 quietly keep if `z'~=.;
 10.  /* delete all observations that don't have a treatment status */;
.                 ** Count the total number of observations;
.         count;
 11.         sca Num_obs=r(N) ;
 12.         sca li Num_obs;
 13.         ** Principal Strata ;
.         quietly gen `at'=1 if `z'==0 & `s'==1;
 14.  quietly replace `at'=0 if `at'==.;
 15.     quietly gen `nt'=1 if `z'==1 & `s'==0;
 16.  quietly replace `nt'=0 if `nt'==.;
 17.     quietly gen `at_c'=1 if `z'==1 & `s'==1;
 18.  quietly replace `at_c'=0 if `at_c'==.;
 19.     quietly gen `nt_c'=1 if `z'==0 & `s'==0;
 20.  quietly replace `nt_c'=0 if `nt_c'==.;
 21.                 **************************************;
.         ** Proportion of Principal Strata ;
.         quietly sum `at' if `z'==0 [aw=`wgt'];
 22.         scalar pr_at=r(mean);
 23.         scalar obs_pr_at=r(N);
 24.         quietly sum `nt' if `z'==1 [aw=`wgt'];
 25.         scalar pr_nt=r(mean);
 26.         scalar obs_pr_nt=r(N);
 27.     quietly sum `at_c' if `z'==1 [aw=`wgt'];
 28.  scalar `pr_at_c'=r(mean);
 29.  scalar obs_pr_at_c=r(N);
 30.         quietly sum `nt_c' if `z'==0 [aw=`wgt'];
 31.  scalar `pr_nt_c'=r(mean);
 32.  scalar obs_pr_nt_c=r(N);
 33.                 scalar pr_c=`pr_at_c'- pr_at;
 34.                 scalar c_11=pr_c/`pr_at_c';
 35.  /* Trimming Proportions */;
.         scalar at_11=pr_at/`pr_at_c';
 36.         scalar c_00=pr_c/`pr_nt_c';
 37.         scalar nt_00=pr_nt/`pr_nt_c';
 38.                 quietly sum `z' [aw=`wgt'];
 39.  scalar pr_z1=r(mean);
 40.  scalar obs_pr_z1=r(N);
 41.         scalar pr_z0=1-r(mean);
 42.  /*Pr(Z=1) and Pr(Z=0)*/;
.                 ****************************************;
.         ** Mean of outcome for each stratum ;
.         quietly sum `y' if `at'==1 [aw=`wgt'];
 43.  scalar y0_at=r(mean);
 44.  scalar obs_y0_at=r(N);
 45.         quietly sum `y' if `at_c'==1 [aw=`wgt'];
 46.  scalar y_at_c=r(mean);
 47.  scalar obs_y_at_c=r(N);
 48.  scalar `sumw1'=r(sum_w);
 49.         quietly sum `y' if `nt'==1 [aw=`wgt'];
 50.  scalar y1_nt=r(mean);
 51.  scalar obs_y1_nt=r(N);
 52.         quietly sum `y' if `nt_c'==1 [aw=`wgt'];
 53.  scalar y_nt_c=r(mean);
 54.  scalar obs_y_nt_c=r(N);
 55.  scalar `sumw0'=r(sum_w);
 56.                 quietly sum `y' if `z'==0 [aw=`wgt'];
 57.  scalar y0=r(mean);
 58.  scalar obs_y0=r(N);
 59.         quietly sum `y' if `z'==1 [aw=`wgt'];
 60.  scalar y1=r(mean);
 61.  scalar obs_y1=r(N);
 62.                 *********************************************;
.         ** Trimming the cell {Z=1,S=1} starts: derive bounds for always-takers and compliers when Z=1.;
.         quietly gen `y_trim1'=`y' if `at_c'==1 ;
 63.         sort `y_trim1' `sv' ;
 64.  /*sort the data.... nonmissing `y' is first */;
.         quietly gen `swgt1'=sum(`wgt') if `at_c'==1 ;
 65.   /* generate running sum of weights */;
.                 ** Lower bound for at;
.                 quietly gen `lowid_at'=1 if `swgt1'<=at_11*`sumw1';
 66.  /* generate variable to indicate lowid_at distribution */;
.                 quietly sum `y_trim1' if `lowid_at'==1 [aw=`wgt'];
 67.  scalar LY1_at=r(mean);
 68.  scalar obs_LY1_at=r(N);
 69.         ** Upper bound for at;
.                 quietly gen `upid_at'=1 if `swgt1'>(1-at_11)*`sumw1';
 70.  /* generate variable to indicate upid_at distribution */;
.                 quietly sum `y_trim1' if `upid_at'==1 [aw=`wgt'];
 71.  scalar UY1_at=r(mean);
 72.  scalar obs_UY1_at=r(N);
 73.                 ** Lower bound for c;
.                 quietly gen `lowid_c1'=1 if `swgt1'<=c_11*`sumw1';
 74.  /* generate variable to indicate lowid_c distribution */;
.                 quietly sum `y_trim1' if `lowid_c1'==1 [aw=`wgt'];
 75.  scalar LY1_c=r(mean);
 76.  scalar obs_LY1_c=r(N);
 77.         ** Upper bound for c;
.                 quietly gen `upid_c1'=1 if `swgt1'>(1-c_11)*`sumw1';
 78.  /* generate variable to indicate upid_c distribution */;
.                 quietly sum `y_trim1' if `upid_c1'==1 [aw=`wgt'];
 79.  scalar UY1_c=r(mean);
 80.  scalar obs_UY1_c=r(N);
 81.                 ** Trimming the cell {Z=0,S=0} starts: derive bounds for never-takers and compliers when Z=0.;
.         quietly gen `y_trim0'=`y' if `nt_c'==1 ;
 82.         sort `y_trim0' `sv' ;
 83. /*sort the data.... nonmissing `y' is first */;
.         quietly gen `swgt0'=sum(`wgt') if `nt_c'==1 ;
 84.  /* generate running sum of weights */;
.                 ** Lower bound for nt;
.                 quietly gen `lowid_nt'=1 if `swgt0'<=nt_00*`sumw0';
 85.  /* generate variable to indicate lowid_nt distribution */;
.                 quietly sum `y_trim0' if `lowid_nt'==1 [aw=`wgt'];
 86.  scalar LY0_nt=r(mean);
 87.  scalar obs_LY0_nt=r(N);
 88.         ** Upper bound for nt;
.                 quietly gen `upid_nt'=1 if `swgt0'>(1-nt_00)*`sumw0';
 89.  /* generate variable to indicate upid_nt distribution */;
.                 quietly sum `y_trim0' if `upid_nt'==1 [aw=`wgt'];
 90.  scalar UY0_nt=r(mean);
 91.  scalar obs_UY0_nt=r(N);
 92.                 ** Lower bound for c;
.                 quietly gen `lowid_c0'=1 if `swgt0'<=c_00*`sumw0';
 93.  /* generate variable to indicate lowid_c distribution */;
.                 quietly sum `y_trim0' if `lowid_c0'==1 [aw=`wgt'];
 94.  scalar LY0_c=r(mean);
 95.  scalar obs_LY0_c=r(N);
 96.         ** Upper bound for c;
.                 quietly gen `upid_c0'=1 if `swgt0'>(1-c_00)*`sumw0';
 97.  /* generate variable to indicate upid_c distribution */;
.                 quietly sum `y_trim0' if `upid_c0'==1 [aw=`wgt'];
 98.  scalar UY0_c=r(mean);
 99.  scalar obs_UY0_c=r(N);
100.                                 ********************************;
.         **Prop1;
.         quietly sum `y' [aw=`wgt'];
101.         scalar miny=r(min);
102.         scalar maxy=r(max);
103.         scalar LB1_0=pr_at*(y0_at-maxy)+`pr_nt_c'*(miny-y_nt_c);
104.         scalar LB1_1=`pr_at_c'*(y_at_c-maxy)+pr_nt*(miny-y1_nt);
105.         scalar UB1_0=pr_at*(y0_at-miny)+`pr_nt_c'*(maxy-y_nt_c);
106.         scalar UB1_1=`pr_at_c'*(y_at_c-miny)+pr_nt*(maxy-y1_nt);
107.                 scalar LB1=pr_z0*LB1_0+pr_z1*LB1_1;
108.         scalar UB1=pr_z0*UB1_0+pr_z1*UB1_1;
109.                 **Prop2;
.         scalar LB2=0;
110.                 scalar UB2_0_1=pr_at*(y0_at-miny)+pr_nt*(maxy-LY0_nt)+y1-y0;
111.         scalar UB2_0_2=pr_at*(y0_at-miny)+pr_nt*(maxy-LY0_nt)+y1-y0-pr_at*(LY1_at-y0_at);
112.         scalar UB2_0_3=pr_at*(y0_at-miny)+pr_nt*(maxy-LY0_nt)+y1-y0-pr_nt*(y1_nt-UY0_nt);
113.         scalar UB2_0_4=pr_at*(y0_at-miny)+pr_nt*(maxy-LY0_nt)+y1-y0-pr_at*(LY1_at-y0_at)-pr_nt*(y1_nt-UY0_nt);
114.         scalar UB2_0_5=pr_at*(y0_at-miny)-`pr_nt_c'*y_nt_c+pr_nt*maxy+pr_c*UY1_c;
115.                 scalar UB2_1_1=pr_at*(UY1_at-miny)+pr_nt*(maxy-y1_nt)+y1-y0;
116.         scalar UB2_1_2=pr_at*(UY1_at-miny)+pr_nt*(maxy-y1_nt)+y1-y0-pr_at*(LY1_at-y0_at);
117.         scalar UB2_1_3=pr_at*(UY1_at-miny)+pr_nt*(maxy-y1_nt)+y1-y0-pr_nt*(y1_nt-UY0_nt);
118.         scalar UB2_1_4=pr_at*(UY1_at-miny)+pr_nt*(maxy-y1_nt)+y1-y0-pr_at*(LY1_at-y0_at)-pr_nt*(y1_nt-UY0_nt);
119.         scalar UB2_1_5=`pr_at_c'*y_at_c+pr_nt*(maxy-y1_nt)-pr_at*miny-pr_c*LY0_c;
120.                 local i=1;
121.         forvalues g=1(1)5{;
122.                 forvalues h=1(1)5{;
123.                 scalar UB2_`i'=pr_z0*UB2_0_`g'+pr_z1*UB2_1_`h';
124.                 local ++i;
125.                 };
126.         };
127.                 **Prop3;
.         scalar LB3_0=y0_at-y_nt_c ;
128.         scalar LB3_1=y_at_c-y1_nt;
129.         scalar UB3_0=pr_at*(y0_at-miny)+pr_nt*maxy-`pr_nt_c'*y_nt_c+pr_c*UY0_nt;
130.         scalar UB3_1=pr_nt*(maxy-y1_nt)-pr_at*miny+`pr_at_c'*y_at_c-pr_c*LY1_at;
131.                 scalar LB3=pr_z0*LB3_0+pr_z1*LB3_1;
132.         scalar UB3=pr_z0*UB3_0+pr_z1*UB3_1;
133.                 **Prop4;
.         scalar LB4=0;
134.                 scalar UB4_0_1=y1-y_nt_c-pr_nt*(LY0_nt-y_at_c);
135.         scalar UB4_0_2=y1-y_nt_c-pr_nt*(LY0_nt-y_at_c+y1_nt-y_nt_c);
136.         scalar UB4_0_3=pr_at*y0_at-y_nt_c+`pr_nt_c'*y_at_c;
137.         scalar UB4_0_4=pr_at*y0_at-y_nt_c+`pr_nt_c'*y0_at;
138.                 scalar UB4_1_1=y_at_c-y0+pr_at*(UY1_at-y_nt_c);
139.         scalar UB4_1_2=y_at_c-y0+pr_at*(UY1_at-y_nt_c-y_at_c+y0_at);
140.         scalar UB4_1_3=y_at_c-pr_nt*y1_nt-`pr_at_c'*y1_nt;
141.         scalar UB4_1_4=y_at_c-pr_nt*y1_nt-`pr_at_c'*y_nt_c;
142.                 local i=1;
143.         forvalues g=1(1)4{;
144.                 forvalues h=1(1)4{;
145.                 scalar UB4_`i'=pr_z0*UB4_0_`g'+pr_z1*UB4_1_`h';
146.                 local ++i;
147.                 };
148.         };
149.         **********************************;
.         **********************************;
.         ** Other values used to calculate Bounds on ATT;
.         quietly sum `s' [aw=`wgt'];
150.  scalar pr_s1=r(mean);
151.  scalar obs_pr_s1=r(N);
152.  /*Pr(S=1)*/;
.         scalar pr_s0=1-r(mean);
153.  /*Pr(S=0)*/;
.         quietly sum `y' if `s'==1 [aw=`wgt'];
154.  scalar ys1=r(mean);
155.  /*E[Y|S=1]*/;
.                 **Prop1 on ATT;
.         sca lb1=ys1-maxy;
156.         sca ub1=ys1-miny;
157.                 **Prop2 on ATT;
.         sca lb2=0;
158.         sca ub2_1=ys1-(pr_z1/pr_s1)*(`pr_nt_c'*y_nt_c-pr_nt*y1_nt)-(pr_at/pr_s1)*miny;
159.         sca ub2_2=ys1-(pr_z1/pr_s1)*pr_c*LY0_c-(pr_at/pr_s1)*miny;
160.                 **Prop3 on ATT;
.         sca lb3=ys1-(pr_z1/pr_s1)*pr_c*UY1_at-(pr_at/pr_s1)*maxy;
161.         sca ub3=ys1-(pr_z1/pr_s1)*`pr_at_c'*y1_nt-(pr_at/pr_s1)*pr_z0*y_nt_c;
162.                 **Prop4 on ATT;
.         sca lb4=0;
163.         sca ub4_1=ys1-(pr_z1/pr_s1)*(`pr_nt_c'*y_nt_c-pr_nt*y1_nt)-(pr_at/pr_s1)*y_nt_c;
164.         sca ub4_2=ys1-(pr_z1/pr_s1)*`pr_at_c'*y1_nt-(pr_at/pr_s1)*pr_z0*y_nt_c;
165.                         **for reference;
.         sca itt=y1-y0;
166.         sca late=itt/pr_c;
167.                         *********************************************;
.         *********************************************;
.         **Local NATE and MATE;
.         **Prop1;
.         **LNATE_nt;
.         sca lb1_nt=y1_nt-UY0_nt;
168.         sca ub1_nt=y1_nt-LY0_nt;
169.     **LNATE_at;
.         sca lb1_at=LY1_at-y0_at ;
170.         sca ub1_at=UY1_at-y0_at ;
171.         **P1: ATE: never-takers ;
.     *Lower bounds ;
.     sca lb1_Ant=pr_z0*(miny-UY0_nt)+pr_z1*(miny-y1_nt);
172.     *Upper bounds ;
.     sca ub1_Ant=pr_z0*(maxy-LY0_nt)+pr_z1*(maxy-y1_nt);
173.         **P1: ATE: always-takers ;
.     *Lower bounds ;
.     sca lb1_Aat=pr_z0*( y0_at-maxy )+pr_z1*( LY1_at-maxy );
174.     *Upper bounds ;
.     sca ub1_Aat=pr_z0*( y0_at-miny )+pr_z1*( UY1_at-miny );
175.         **Prop2;
.         **LNATE_nt;
.         sca lb2_nt_1=0;
176.         sca lb2_nt_2=y1_nt-UY0_nt;
177.         sca ub2_nt=y1_nt-LY0_nt;
178.         **LNATE_at;
.         sca lb2_at_1=0;
179.         sca lb2_at_2=LY1_at-y0_at;
180.         sca ub2_at=UY1_at-y0_at;
181.         **LNATE_c0, LNATE_c1, LMATE_c1, LMATE_c0 (they are all the same);
.         sca lb2_c=0;
182.         sca ub2_c=UY1_c-LY0_c;
183.         ** MATE;
.     sca ub2_M_1 = y1 - y0 ;
184.      sca ub2_M_2 = y1 - y0 - (pr_at * (LY1_at - y0_at)) ;
185.      sca ub2_M_3 = y1 - y0 - (pr_nt * (y1_nt - UY0_nt)) ;
186.      sca ub2_M_4 = y1 - y0 - (pr_at * (LY1_at - y0_at)) - (pr_nt * (y1_nt - UY0_nt)) ;
187.         sca lb2_M = 0;
188.         ** NATE;
.         sca lb2_N_1 = y1 - y0 - ub2_M_1 ;
189.      sca lb2_N_2 = y1 - y0 - ub2_M_2 ;
190.      sca lb2_N_3 = y1 - y0 - ub2_M_3 ;
191.      sca lb2_N_4 = y1 - y0 - ub2_M_4 ;
192.         sca ub2_N_4 = y1 - y0 ;
193.         ** LATE;
.         sca lb2_L = lb2_M /pr_c ;
194.      sca ub2_L_1 = ub2_M_1 /pr_c ;
195.      sca ub2_L_2 = ub2_M_2 /pr_c ;
196.      sca ub2_L_3 = ub2_M_3 /pr_c ;
197.      sca ub2_L_4 = ub2_M_4 /pr_c ;
198.         **LATE_nt ;
.         sca lb2_Ant=0;
199.         sca ub2_Ant=pr_z1*(maxy-y1_nt)+pr_z0*(maxy-LY0_nt);
200.         **LATE_at ;
.         sca lb2_Aat=0;
201.         sca ub2_Aat=pr_z1*(UY1_at-miny)+pr_z0*(y0_at-miny);
202.                         **Prop3;
.         **LNATE_nt;
.         sca lb3_nt = y1_nt-y_nt_c;
203.         sca ub3_nt = y1_nt-LY0_nt;
204.         **LNATE_at;
.         sca lb3_at = y_at_c-y0_at;
205.         sca ub3_at = UY1_at-y0_at;
206.         **LNATE_c0;
.         sca lb3_cN0_1 = y1_nt-UY0_c;
207.         sca lb3_cN0_2 = y1_nt-y0_at;
208.         sca ub3_cN0 = UY1_at-y_nt_c;
209.         **LNATE_c1;
.         sca lb3_cN1_1 = LY1_c-y0_at;
210.         sca lb3_cN1_2 = y1_nt-y0_at;
211.         sca ub3_cN1 = y_at_c-LY0_nt;
212.         **LMATE_c1;
.         sca lb3_cM1_1 = LY1_c-UY1_at;
213.         sca lb3_cM1_2 = y1_nt-UY1_at;
214.         sca ub3_cM1 = y_at_c-y1_nt;
215.         **LMATE_c0;
.         sca lb3_cM0_1 = LY0_nt-UY0_c;
216.         sca lb3_cM0_2 = LY0_nt-y0_at;
217.         sca ub3_cM0 = y0_at-y_nt_c;
218.         ** MATE;
.         sca lb3_M_1 = pr_c * (LY1_c-UY1_at);
219.     sca lb3_M_2 = pr_c * (y1_nt-UY1_at);
220.         sca ub3_M = pr_c * (y_at_c-y1_nt);
221.         ** NATE;
.         sca lb3_N = y1-y0 - ub3_M;
222.      sca ub3_N_1 = y1-y0 - lb3_M_1;
223.      sca ub3_N_2 = y1-y0 - lb3_M_2;
224.         ** LATE;
.         sca lb3_L_1 = lb3_M_1/pr_c;
225.      sca lb3_L_2 = lb3_M_2/pr_c;
226.         sca ub3_L = ub3_M/pr_c;
227.         **LATE_nt ;
.         sca lb3_Ant=pr_z1*(miny-y1_nt)+pr_z0*(miny-y_nt_c);
228.         sca ub3_Ant=pr_z1*(y_at_c-y1_nt)+pr_z0*(y0_at-LY0_nt);
229.         **LATE_at ;
.         sca lb3_Aat=pr_z1*(y_at_c-maxy)+pr_z0*(y0_at-maxy);
230.         sca ub3_Aat=pr_z1*(UY1_at-y1_nt)+pr_z0*(y0_at-y_nt_c);
231.                                 **Prop4;
.         **LNATE_nt;
.         sca lb4_nt_1=0;
232.         sca lb4_nt_2=y1_nt-y_nt_c;
233.         sca ub4_nt=y1_nt-LY0_nt;
234.         **LNATE_at;
.         sca lb4_at_1=0;
235.         sca lb4_at_2=y_at_c-y0_at;
236.         sca ub4_at=UY1_at-y0_at;
237.         **LNATE_c0;
.         sca lb4_cN0_1=y1_nt-UY0_c;
238.         sca lb4_cN0_2=y1_nt-y0_at;
239.         sca lb4_cN0_3=0;
240.         sca ub4_cN0=y_at_c-y_nt_c;
241.         **LNATE_c1;
.         sca lb4_cN1_1=LY1_c-y0_at;
242.         sca lb4_cN1_2=y1_nt-y0_at;
243.         sca lb4_cN1_3=0;
244.         sca ub4_cN1=y_at_c-y_nt_c;
245.         **LMATE_c1;
.         sca lb4_cM1=0;
246.         sca ub4_cM1_1=y_at_c-y1_nt;
247.         sca ub4_cM1_2=y_at_c-y_nt_c;
248.         **LMATE_c0;
.         sca lb4_cM0=0;
249.         sca ub4_cM0_1=y0_at-y_nt_c;
250.         sca ub4_cM0_2=y_at_c-y_nt_c;
251.         ** MATE;
.         sca lb4_M = 0 ;
252.             sca ub4_M_1 = y1 - pr_at * y_at_c - pr_nt * y1_nt - pr_c * y1_nt;
253.         sca ub4_M_2 = y1 - pr_at * y0_at - pr_nt * y1_nt - pr_c * y1_nt;
254.         sca ub4_M_3 = y1 - pr_at * y_at_c - pr_nt * y1_nt - pr_c * y_nt_c;
255.         sca ub4_M_4 = y1 - pr_at * y0_at - pr_nt * y1_nt - pr_c * y_nt_c;
256.                 sca ub4_M_5 = y1 - y0 - pr_at*0 - pr_nt*0 - pr_c*0;
257.         sca ub4_M_6 = y1 - y0 - pr_at*lb4_at_2 - pr_nt*0 - pr_c*0;
258.         sca ub4_M_7 = y1 - y0 - pr_at*0 - pr_nt*lb4_nt_2 - pr_c*0;
259.         sca ub4_M_8 = y1 - y0 - pr_at*lb4_at_2 - pr_nt*lb4_nt_2- pr_c*0;
260.                 sca ub4_M_9 = y1 - y0 - pr_at*0 - pr_nt*0 - pr_c*lb4_cN0_1;
261.         sca ub4_M_10 = y1 - y0 - pr_at*lb4_at_2 - pr_nt*0 - pr_c*lb4_cN0_1;
262.         sca ub4_M_11 = y1 - y0 - pr_at*0 - pr_nt*lb4_nt_2 - pr_c*lb4_cN0_1;
263.         sca ub4_M_12 = y1 - y0 - pr_at*lb4_at_2 - pr_nt*lb4_nt_2- pr_c*lb4_cN0_1;
264.                 sca ub4_M_13 = y1 - y0 - pr_at*0 - pr_nt*0 - pr_c*lb4_cN0_2;
265.         sca ub4_M_14 = y1 - y0 - pr_at*lb4_at_2 - pr_nt*0 - pr_c*lb4_cN0_2;
266.         sca ub4_M_15 = y1 - y0 - pr_at*0 - pr_nt*lb4_nt_2 - pr_c*lb4_cN0_2;
267.         sca ub4_M_16 = y1 - y0 - pr_at*lb4_at_2 - pr_nt*lb4_nt_2- pr_c*lb4_cN0_2;
268.                 ** NATE;
.         sca lb4_N_1 = y1 - y0 - ub4_M_1;
269.         sca lb4_N_2 = y1 - y0 - ub4_M_2;
270.         sca lb4_N_3 = y1 - y0 - ub4_M_3;
271.         sca lb4_N_4 = y1 - y0 - ub4_M_4;
272.                 sca lb4_N_5 = y1 - y0 - ub4_M_5;
273.         sca lb4_N_6 = y1 - y0 - ub4_M_6;
274.         sca lb4_N_7 = y1 - y0 - ub4_M_7;
275.         sca lb4_N_8 = y1 - y0 - ub4_M_8;
276.                 sca lb4_N_9 = y1 - y0 - ub4_M_9;
277.         sca lb4_N_10 = y1 - y0 - ub4_M_10;
278.         sca lb4_N_11 = y1 - y0 - ub4_M_11;
279.         sca lb4_N_12 = y1 - y0 - ub4_M_12;
280.                 sca lb4_N_13 = y1 - y0 - ub4_M_13;
281.         sca lb4_N_14 = y1 - y0 - ub4_M_14;
282.         sca lb4_N_15 = y1 - y0 - ub4_M_15;
283.         sca lb4_N_16 = y1 - y0 - ub4_M_16;
284.                 sca ub4_N = y1 - y0;
285.                 ** LATE;
.         sca lb4_L = lb4_M/pr_c;
286.             sca ub4_L_1 = ub4_M_1/pr_c;
287.         sca ub4_L_2 = ub4_M_2/pr_c;
288.         sca ub4_L_3 = ub4_M_3/pr_c;
289.         sca ub4_L_4 = ub4_M_4/pr_c;
290.                 sca ub4_L_5 = ub4_M_5/pr_c;
291.         sca ub4_L_6 = ub4_M_6/pr_c;
292.         sca ub4_L_7 = ub4_M_7/pr_c;
293.         sca ub4_L_8 = ub4_M_8/pr_c;
294.                 sca ub4_L_9 = ub4_M_9/pr_c;
295.         sca ub4_L_10 = ub4_M_10/pr_c;
296.         sca ub4_L_11 = ub4_M_11/pr_c;
297.         sca ub4_L_12 = ub4_M_12/pr_c;
298.                 sca ub4_L_13 = ub4_M_13/pr_c;
299.         sca ub4_L_14 = ub4_M_14/pr_c;
300.         sca ub4_L_15 = ub4_M_15/pr_c;
301.         sca ub4_L_16 = ub4_M_16/pr_c;
302.                 **LATE_nt ;
.         sca lb4_Ant=pr_z1*0+pr_z0*0;
303.         sca ub4_Ant_1=pr_z1*(y_at_c-y1_nt)+pr_z0*(y0_at-LY0_nt);
304.         sca ub4_Ant_2=pr_z1*(y_at_c-y1_nt)+pr_z0*(y_at_c-LY0_nt);
305.         **LATE_at ;
.         sca lb4_Aat=pr_z1*0+pr_z0*0;
306.         sca ub4_Aat_1=pr_z1*(UY1_at-y1_nt)+pr_z0*(y0_at-y_nt_c);
307.         sca ub4_Aat_2=pr_z1*(UY1_at-y_nt_c)+pr_z0*(y0_at-y_nt_c);
308.                 ** Conditional Probabilities ;
.         sca itt=y1-y0;
309.         sca li itt;
310.                 ** Testable implications ;
.         sca imp_a=y0_at-y_nt_c;
311.         sca li imp_a;
312.                 sca imp_b=y1_nt-y_at_c;
313.         sca li imp_b;
314.             sca imp_c=y_at_c-y_nt_c;
315.         sca li imp_c;
316.                 ** Mean of y on s;
.         sum `y' if `s'==1 [aw=`wgt'];
317.         sca y_s1=r(mean);
318.  sca obs_y_s1=r(N);
319.         sum `y' if `s'==0 [aw=`wgt'];
320.         sca y_s0=r(mean);
321.  sca obs_y_s0=r(N);
322.                 ** Percentage of LNATE_nt;
.         sca L_perc_lnate=(y1_nt-UY0_nt)/UY0_nt;
323.         sca U_perc_lnate=1;
324.         sca li U_perc_lnate;
325.         matrix b_all_1= (Num_obs, itt, pr_c, late, pr_at, pr_nt, `pr_at_c', `pr_nt_c', 
>                        y_at_c, y_nt_c, y0_at, y1_nt, y1, y0, y_s1, y_s0, imp_a,
